I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
会话锁导致并发消息丢弃：连续发送多条消息只处理第一条
## 问题描述

当用户快速连续发送多条消息（如多张图片）时，cc-connect 只处理第一条，其余消息在会话锁定期间被静默丢弃，session 解锁后也不会补处理。

## 日志证据

```
20:45:17.184 downloaded image  size=244513   ← 第1张，成功下载
20:45:17.184 processing message              ← 第1张，进入处理
20:45:17.195 interactive session started     ← session 被锁
20:45:17.389 message received                ← 第2张消息到达
20:45:17.916 downloaded image  size=266337   ← 第2张，成功下载
20:45:18.003 message received                ← 第3张消息到达
20:45:18.629 downloaded image  size=680155   ← 第3张，成功下载
20:45:47.738 turn complete                   ← 第1张处理完毕
（之后无任何 processing message — 第2、3张被丢弃）
```

## 使用场景

报销场景中员工需要一次性发送多张发票/付款截图。当前只能逐张发送并等待机器人回复后再发下一张，体验很差。

## 期望行为

会话锁定期间收到的消息应该排队等待，session 解锁后依次处理，而不是丢弃。

## 环境

- cc-connect 版本：1.2.1
- 平台：feishu（WebSocket 模式）
- Agent：claudecode

</pr_description>

   294	func (s *interactiveState) stopSignal() <-chan struct{} {
   295	        s.mu.Lock()
   296	        defer s.mu.Unlock()
   297	        if s.stopCh == nil {
   298	                s.stopCh = make(chan struct{})
   299	                if s.stopped {
   300	                        close(s.stopCh)
   301	                }
   302	        }
   303	        return s.stopCh
   304	}
   305	
   306	func (s *interactiveState) isStopped() bool {
   307	        s.mu.Lock()
   308	        defer s.mu.Unlock()
   309	        return s.stopped
   310	}

  1470	        session := sessions.GetOrCreateActive(msg.SessionKey)
  1471	        sessions.UpdateUserMeta(msg.SessionKey, msg.UserName, msg.ChatName)
  1472	        if !session.TryLock() {
  1473	                // Check for /btw — inject into the running session mid-turn
  1474	                trimmed := strings.TrimSpace(content)
  1475	                if isBtwCommand(trimmed) {
  1476	                        btw := strings.TrimSpace(trimmed[len(matchBtwPrefix(trimmed)):])
  1477	                        if btw != "" {
  1478	                                e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  1479	                                state, ok := e.interactiveStates[interactiveKey]
  1480	                                e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  1481	                                if ok && state.agentSession != nil && state.agentSession.Alive() {
  1482	                                        if err := state.agentSession.Send(btw, nil, nil); err != nil {
  1483	                                                slog.Error("btw: send failed", "error", err)
  1484	                                                e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgBtwSendFailed))
  1485	                                        } else {
  1486	                                                e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgBtwSent))
  1487	                                        }
  1488	                                        return
  1489	                                }
  1490	                        }
  1491	                }
  1492	                // Session is busy — try to queue the message for the running turn
  1493	                // so the agent processes it immediately after the current turn ends.
  1494	                if e.queueMessageForBusySession(p, msg, interactiveKey) {
  1495	                        // Race guard: the drain loop in processInteractiveMessageWith may
  1496	                        // have just finished (session unlocked) between our TryLock failure
  1497	                        // and the queue append. Re-try TryLock — if it succeeds, no one is
  1498	                        // draining the queue so we must start a processor ourselves.
  1499	                        if session.TryLock() {
  1500	                                go e.drainOrphanedQueue(session, sessions, interactiveKey, agent, resolvedWorkspace)
  1501	                        }
  1502	                        return
  1503	                }
  1504	                e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgPreviousProcessing))
  1505	                return
  1506	        }
  1507	
  1508	        if rotated := e.maybeAutoResetSessionOnIdle(p, msg, sessions, interactiveKey, session); rotated != nil {
  1509	                session = rotated
  1510	        }
  1511	
  1512	        slog.Info("processing message",
  1513	                "platform", msg.Platform,
  1514	                "user", msg.UserName,
  1515	                "session", session.ID,
  1516	        )
  1517	
  1518	        go e.processInteractiveMessageWith(p, msg, session, agent, sessions, interactiveKey, resolvedWorkspace, msg.SessionKey)
  1519	}
  1520	
  1521	func (e *Engine) maybeAutoResetSessionOnIdle(p Platform, msg *Message, sessions *SessionManager, interactiveKey string, session *Session) *Session {
  1522	        if e.resetOnIdle <= 0 || session == nil {
  1523	                return nil
  1524	        }
  1525	
  1526	        hasBackend := session.GetAgentSessionID() != ""
  1527	        hasHistory := len(session.GetHistory(1)) > 0
  1528	        if !hasBackend && !hasHistory {
  1529	                return nil
  1530	        }
  1531	
  1532	        lastActive := session.GetUpdatedAt()
  1533	        if lastActive.IsZero() || time.Since(lastActive) < e.resetOnIdle {
  1534	                return nil
  1535	        }
  1536	
  1537	        slog.Info("auto-resetting idle session",
  1538	                "session_key", msg.SessionKey,
  1539	                "session_id", session.ID,
  1540	                "idle_for", time.Since(lastActive),
  1541	                "threshold", e.resetOnIdle,
  1542	        )
  1543	
  1544	        // Check if the old session has an agent process that needs graceful
  1545	        // shutdown. If so, tell the user we're wrapping up before blocking.
  1546	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  1547	        state, hasState := e.interactiveStates[interactiveKey]
  1548	        hasAgent := hasState && state != nil && state.agentSession != nil && state.agentSession.Alive()
  1549	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  1550	
  1551	        if hasAgent {
  1552	                // Notify the user before the potentially long close. The close
  1553	                // returns as soon as the process exits (usually seconds), but
  1554	                // Stop hooks can take up to 120s.
  1555	                e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgSessionClosingGraceful))
  1556	        }
  1557	
  1558	        e.cleanupInteractiveState(interactiveKey)
  1559	        session.UnlockWithoutUpdate()
  1560	
  1561	        newSession := sessions.NewSession(msg.SessionKey, "")
  1562	        if !newSession.TryLock() {
  1563	                slog.Error("failed to lock new session after idle auto-reset", "session_key", msg.SessionKey, "new_session", newSession.ID)
  1564	                return nil
  1565	        }
  1566	
  1567	        e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.Tf(MsgSessionAutoResetIdle, int(e.resetOnIdle/time.Minute)))
  1568	        return newSession
  1569	}
  1570	
  1571	// queueMessageForBusySession queues a message for later delivery when the
  1572	// session is busy. The message is NOT sent to agent stdin at queue time;
  1573	// the event loop sends it after the current turn's EventResult is received.
  1574	// Returns true if the message was successfully queued, false otherwise.
  1575	func (e *Engine) queueMessageForBusySession(p Platform, msg *Message, interactiveKey string) bool {
  1576	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  1577	        state, hasState := e.interactiveStates[interactiveKey]
  1578	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  1579	
  1580	        if !hasState || state == nil || state.agentSession == nil || !state.agentSession.Alive() {
  1581	                return false
  1582	        }
  1583	
  1584	        // Only queue metadata — do NOT send to agent stdin yet.
  1585	        // The agent CLI may treat a mid-turn stdin message as part of the
  1586	        // current turn, causing the event loop to hang waiting for a second
  1587	        // EventResult that never arrives. Instead, the event loop sends the
  1588	        // message after the current turn's EventResult is received.
  1589	        state.mu.Lock()
  1590	        if len(state.pendingMessages) >= maxQueuedMessages {
  1591	                state.mu.Unlock()
  1592	                return false // fall back to "previous processing" reply
  1593	        }
  1594	        state.pendingMessages = append(state.pendingMessages, queuedMessage{
  1595	                platform:      p,
  1596	                replyCtx:      msg.ReplyCtx,
  1597	                content:       msg.Content,
  1598	                images:        msg.Images,
  1599	                files:         msg.Files,
  1600	                fromVoice:     msg.FromVoice,
  1601	                userID:        msg.UserID,
  1602	                msgPlatform:   msg.Platform,
  1603	                msgSessionKey: msg.SessionKey,
  1604	        })
  1605	        queueDepth := len(state.pendingMessages)
  1606	        state.mu.Unlock()
  1607	
  1608	        slog.Info("message queued for busy session",
  1609	                "session", msg.SessionKey,
  1610	                "user", msg.UserName,
  1611	                "queue_depth", queueDepth,
  1612	        )
  1613	        e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgMessageQueued))
  1614	        return true
  1615	}
  1616	
  1617	// drainOrphanedQueue is called when a message was queued but the drain loop
  1618	// has already exited. It processes all pending messages in the state, similar
  1619	// to the drain loop in processInteractiveMessageWith but as a standalone
  1620	// goroutine.
  1621	func (e *Engine) drainOrphanedQueue(session *Session, sessions *SessionManager, interactiveKey string, agent Agent, workspaceDir string) {
  1622	        unlocked := false
  1623	        defer func() {
  1624	                if !unlocked {
  1625	                        session.Unlock()
  1626	                }
  1627	        }()
  1628	
  1629	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  1630	        state, hasState := e.interactiveStates[interactiveKey]
  1631	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  1632	
  1633	        if !hasState || state == nil || state.agentSession == nil || !state.agentSession.Alive() {
  1634	                if hasState && state != nil {
  1635	                        e.notifyDroppedQueuedMessages(state, fmt.Errorf("agent session ended"))
  1636	                }
  1637	                return
  1638	        }
  1639	
  1640	        unlocked = e.drainPendingMessages(state, session, sessions, interactiveKey)
  1641	}
  1642	
  1643	// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  1644	// Voice message handling
  1645	// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  1647	func (e *Engine) handleVoiceMessage(p Platform, msg *Message) {
  1648	        if !e.speech.Enabled || e.speech.STT == nil {
  1649	                e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgVoiceNotEnabled))
  1650	                return
  1651	        }
  1652	
  1653	        audio := msg.Audio
  1654	        if NeedsConversion(audio.Format) && !HasFFmpeg() {
  1655	                e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgVoiceNoFFmpeg))
  1656	                return
  1657	        }
  1658	
  1659	        slog.Info("transcribing voice message",
  1660	                "platform", msg.Platform, "user", msg.UserName,
  1661	                "format", audio.Format, "size", len(audio.Data),
  1662	        )
  1663	        e.send(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgVoiceTranscribing))
  1664	
  1665	        text, err := TranscribeAudio(e.ctx, e.speech.STT, audio, e.speech.Language)

  1885	// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  1886	// Interactive agent processing
  1887	// ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  1888	
  1889	func (e *Engine) processInteractiveMessage(p Platform, msg *Message, session *Session) {
  1890	        e.processInteractiveMessageWith(p, msg, session, e.agent, e.sessions, msg.SessionKey, "", "")
  1891	}
  1892	
  1893	// processInteractiveMessageWith is the core interactive processing loop.
  1894	// It accepts an explicit agent, interactiveKey (for the interactiveStates map),
  1895	// and workspaceDir so that multi-workspace mode can route to per-workspace agents.
  1896	// ccSessionKey, when non-empty, is used for CC_SESSION_KEY in the agent env; otherwise interactiveKey is used.
  1897	func (e *Engine) processInteractiveMessageWith(p Platform, msg *Message, session *Session, agent Agent, sessions *SessionManager, interactiveKey string, workspaceDir string, ccSessionKey string) {
  1898	        // session.Unlock() is NOT deferred here — it is called explicitly in
  1899	        // the drain loop below while holding state.mu to close the race window
  1900	        // between "queue is empty" and "session unlocked". A deferred fallback
  1901	        // ensures the lock is released on early-return paths.
  1902	        unlocked := false
  1903	        defer func() {
  1904	                if !unlocked {
  1905	                        session.Unlock()
  1906	                }
  1907	        }()
  1908	
  1909	        if e.ctx.Err() != nil {
  1910	                return
  1911	        }
  1912	
  1913	        turnStart := time.Now()
  1914	
  1915	        e.i18n.DetectAndSet(msg.Content)
  1916	        session.AddHistory("user", msg.Content)
  1917	
  1918	        // Use the agent override when available (multi-workspace mode)
  1919	        var agentOverride Agent
  1920	        if agent != e.agent {
  1921	                agentOverride = agent
  1922	        }
  1923	        state := e.getOrCreateInteractiveStateWith(interactiveKey, p, msg.ReplyCtx, session, sessions, agentOverride, ccSessionKey)
  1924	
  1925	        // Set workspaceDir on the state for idle reaper identification
  1926	        if workspaceDir != "" {
  1927	                state.mu.Lock()
  1928	                state.workspaceDir = workspaceDir
  1929	                state.mu.Unlock()
  1930	        }
  1931	
  1932	        // Update reply context for this turn
  1933	        state.mu.Lock()
  1934	        state.platform = p
  1935	        state.replyCtx = msg.ReplyCtx
  1936	        state.mu.Unlock()
  1937	
  1938	        if state.agentSession == nil {
  1939	                e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgFailedToStartAgentSession))
  1940	                return
  1941	        }
  1942	
  1943	        if workspaceDir != "" && e.workspacePool != nil {
  1944	                ws := e.workspacePool.GetOrCreate(workspaceDir)
  1945	                ws.BeginTurn()
  1946	                defer ws.EndTurn()
  1947	        }
  1948	
  1949	        // Apply per-message permission mode override (e.g. cron jobs with mode = "bypassPermissions").
  1950	        // Defer restores only when SetLiveMode succeeds for the override.
  1951	        if msg.ModeOverride != "" {
  1952	                if switcher, ok := state.agentSession.(LiveModeSwitcher); ok {
  1953	                        if switcher.SetLiveMode(msg.ModeOverride) {
  1954	                                defer func() {
  1955	                                        defaultMode := "default"
  1956	                                        if ma, ok := e.agent.(interface{ GetMode() string }); ok {
  1957	                                                if m := ma.GetMode(); m != "" {
  1958	                                                        defaultMode = m
  1959	                                                }
  1960	                                        }
  1961	                                        switcher.SetLiveMode(defaultMode)
  1962	                                }()
  1963	                        }
  1964	                }
  1965	        }
  1966	
  1967	        // Start typing indicator if platform supports it.
  1968	        // Ownership is transferred to processInteractiveEvents which manages
  1969	        // stopping/restarting it across queued message turns.
  1970	        var stopTyping func()
  1971	        if ti, ok := p.(TypingIndicator); ok {
  1972	                stopTyping = ti.StartTyping(e.ctx, msg.ReplyCtx)
  1973	        }
  1974	        defer func() {
  1975	                // Stop typing if ownership was NOT transferred to processInteractiveEvents
  1976	                // (i.e. an early return before that call).
  1977	                if stopTyping != nil {
  1978	                        stopTyping()
  1979	                }
  1980	        }()
  1981	
  1982	        // Drain any stale events left in the channel from a previous turn.
  1983	        // This prevents the next processInteractiveEvents from reading an old
  1984	        // EventResult that was pushed after the previous turn already returned.
  1985	        drainEvents(state.agentSession.Events())
  1986	
  1987	        promptContent := e.buildSenderPrompt(msg.Content, msg.UserID, msg.Platform, msg.SessionKey)
  1988	
  1989	        sendStart := time.Now()
  1990	        state.mu.Lock()
  1991	        state.fromVoice = msg.FromVoice
  1992	        state.sideText = ""
  1993	        state.mu.Unlock()
  1994	
  1995	        // Run Send concurrently with processInteractiveEvents. Some agents block inside
  1996	        // Send until the prompt turn finishes (e.g. ACP session/prompt); they may emit
  1997	        // EventPermissionRequest while blocked — the event loop must run in parallel.
  1998	        sendDone := make(chan error, 1)
  1999	        go func() {
  2000	                sendDone <- state.agentSession.Send(promptContent, msg.Images, msg.Files)
  2001	        }()
  2002	
  2003	        e.processInteractiveEvents(state, session, sessions, interactiveKey, msg.MessageID, turnStart, stopTyping, sendDone, msg.ReplyCtx)
  2004	        if elapsed := time.Since(sendStart); elapsed >= slowAgentSend {
  2005	                slog.Warn("slow agent send", "elapsed", elapsed, "session", msg.SessionKey, "content_len", len(msg.Content))
  2006	        }
  2007	        stopTyping = nil // ownership transferred; prevent defer from double-stopping
  2008	
  2009	        // Guard against a narrow race: a message may have been queued between
  2010	        // processInteractiveEvents observing an empty queue and returning here
  2011	        // (session is still locked, so handleMessage's TryLock fails and routes
  2012	        // the message to queueMessageForBusySession). Drain any such orphans.
  2013	        if e.drainPendingMessages(state, session, sessions, interactiveKey) {
  2014	                unlocked = true
  2015	        }
  2016	}

  2026	                return ws.agent, ws.sessions, nil
  2027	        }

  2030	        opts := make(map[string]any)

  1324	func (e *Engine) handleMessage(p Platform, msg *Message) {
  1325	        slog.Info("message received",
  1326	                "platform", msg.Platform, "msg_id", msg.MessageID,
  1327	                "session", msg.SessionKey, "user", msg.UserName,
  1328	                "content_len", len(msg.Content),
  1329	                "has_images", len(msg.Images) > 0, "has_audio", msg.Audio != nil, "has_files", len(msg.Files) > 0,
  1330	        )
  1331	
  1332	        // Voice message: transcribe to text first
  1333	        if msg.Audio != nil {
  1334	                // If STT is configured, use it for transcription (more accurate)
  1335	                if e.speech.Enabled && e.speech.STT != nil {
  1336	                        e.handleVoiceMessage(p, msg)
  1337	                        return
  1338	                }
  1339	                // Fallback: use platform-provided recognition text if available
  1340	                if msg.Content == "" {
  1341	                        e.reply(p, msg.ReplyCtx, e.i18n.T(MsgVoiceNotEnabled))
  1342	                        return
  1343	                }
  1344	                // Use platform recognition with a hint, then continue processing
  1345	                slog.Info("using platform-provided voice recognition",
  1346	                        "platform", msg.Platform, "content_len", len(msg.Content))
  1347	                if msg.FromVoice {
  1348	                        // Use platform name as parameter for the message
  1349	                        // Capitalize first letter for better presentation
  1350	                        if platformName := msg.Platform; len(platformName) > 0 {
  1351	                                // Safe capitalization that handles multi-word names
  1352	                                r := []rune(platformName)
  1353	                                if len(r) > 0 {
  1354	                                        r[0] = []rune(strings.ToUpper(string(r[0])))[0]
  1355	                                }
  1356	                                platformName = string(r)

  2115	// When agentOverride is non-nil it is used instead of e.agent to start the session.
  2116	// ccSessionKey, when non-empty, is used for CC_SESSION_KEY env injection; otherwise sessionKey is used.
  2117	func (e *Engine) getOrCreateInteractiveStateWith(sessionKey string, p Platform, replyCtx any, session *Session, sessions *SessionManager, agentOverride Agent, ccSessionKey string) *interactiveState {

  2120	
  2121	        state, ok := e.interactiveStates[sessionKey]
  2122	        if ok && state.agentSession != nil && state.agentSession.Alive() {
  2123	                // Verify the running agent session matches the current active session.
  2124	                // After /new or /switch the active session changes, but the old agent
  2125	                // process may still be alive. Reusing it would send messages to the
  2126	                // wrong conversation context.

  2927	// drainPendingMessages processes all queued messages in the state's pendingMessages
  2928	// queue. It atomically unlocks the session when the queue is empty (while holding
  2929	// state.mu) to close the race window between "queue empty" and "session unlocked".
  2930	// Returns true if the session was unlocked by this call.
  2931	func (e *Engine) drainPendingMessages(state *interactiveState, session *Session, sessions *SessionManager, sessionKey string) bool {
  2932	        for {
  2933	                state.mu.Lock()
  2934	                if len(state.pendingMessages) == 0 {
  2935	                        session.Unlock()
  2936	                        state.mu.Unlock()
  2937	                        return true
  2938	                }
  2939	                queued := state.pendingMessages[0]
  2940	                state.pendingMessages = state.pendingMessages[1:]
  2941	                state.platform = queued.platform
  2942	                state.replyCtx = queued.replyCtx
  2943	                state.fromVoice = queued.fromVoice
  2944	                state.mu.Unlock()
  2945

  2947	                prompt := e.buildSenderPrompt(queued.content, queued.userID, queued.msgPlatform, queued.msgSessionKey)
  2948	
  2949	                if state.agentSession == nil || !state.agentSession.Alive() {
  2950	                        e.send(queued.platform, queued.replyCtx, fmt.Sprintf(e.i18n.T(MsgError), "agent session ended"))
  2951	                        e.notifyDroppedQueuedMessages(state, fmt.Errorf("agent session ended"))
  2952	                        return false
  2953	                }
  2954	
  2955	                drainEvents(state.agentSession.Events())
  2956

  2967	                }

     1	package core
     2	
     3	import (
     4	        "encoding/json"
     5	        "fmt"
     6	        "log/slog"
     7	        "os"
     8	        "path/filepath"
     9	        "sync"
    10	        "time"
    11	)
    12	
    13	// ContinueSession is a sentinel value for AgentSessionID that tells the agent
    14	// to use --continue (resume most recent session) instead of a specific session ID.
    15	const ContinueSession = "__continue__"
    16	
    17	// Session tracks one conversation between a user and the agent.
    18	type Session struct {
    19	        ID             string         `json:"id"`
    20	        Name           string         `json:"name"`
    21	        AgentSessionID string         `json:"agent_session_id"`
    22	        AgentType      string         `json:"agent_type,omitempty"`
    23	        History        []HistoryEntry `json:"history"`
    24	        CreatedAt      time.Time      `json:"created_at"`
    25	        UpdatedAt      time.Time      `json:"updated_at"`
    26	
    27	        mu   sync.Mutex `json:"-"`
    28	        busy bool       `json:"-"`
    29	}
    30	
    31	func (s *Session) TryLock() bool {
    32	        s.mu.Lock()
    33	        defer s.mu.Unlock()
    34	        if s.busy {
    35	                return false
    36	        }
    37	        s.busy = true
    38	        return true
    39	}
    40	
    41	func (s *Session) Unlock() {
    42	        s.unlock(true)
    43	}
    44	
    45	func (s *Session) UnlockWithoutUpdate() {
    46	        s.unlock(false)
    47	}
    48	
    49	func (s *Session) unlock(update bool) {
    50	        s.mu.Lock()
    51	        defer s.mu.Unlock()
    52	        s.busy = false
    53	        if update {
    54	                s.UpdatedAt = time.Now()
    55	        }
    56	}
    57	
    58	func (s *Session) AddHistory(role, content string) {
    59	        s.mu.Lock()
    60	        defer s.mu.Unlock()
    61	        s.History = append(s.History, HistoryEntry{
    62	                Role:      role,
    63	                Content:   content,
    64	                Timestamp: time.Now(),
    65	        })
    66	}
    67	
    68	// SetAgentInfo atomically sets the agent session ID, agent type, and name.
    69	func (s *Session) SetAgentInfo(agentSessionID, agentType, name string) {
    70	        if agentSessionID == ContinueSession {
    71	                agentSessionID = ""
    72	        }
    73	        s.mu.Lock()
    74	        defer s.mu.Unlock()
    75	        s.AgentSessionID = agentSessionID
    76	        s.AgentType = agentType
    77	        s.Name = name
    78	}
    79

   750	
   751	// dispatchMessage handles the message content parsing, media download, and
   752	// handler invocation. It runs in its own goroutine so that onMessage returns
   753	// quickly and does not block the SDK event loop.
   754	func (p *Platform) dispatchMessage(ctx context.Context, msgType, content string, mentions []*larkim.MentionEvent, messageID, sessionKey, userID, userName, chatName string, rctx replyContext, parentID string) {
   755	        // If this message is a reply to another message, fetch the quoted content
   756	        // and prepend it so the agent has full context.
   757	        quotedPrefix := ""
   758	        if parentID != "" {
   759	                quotedPrefix = p.fetchQuotedMessage(ctx, parentID)
   760	        }
   761	
   762	        switch msgType {
   763	        case "text":
   764	                var textBody struct {
   765	                        Text string `json:"text"`
   766	                }
   767	                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(content), &textBody); err != nil {
   768	                        slog.Error(p.tag()+": failed to parse text content", "error", err)
   769	                        return
   770	                }
   771	                text := stripMentions(textBody.Text, mentions, p.botOpenID)
   772	                if text == "" {
   773	                        slog.Debug(p.tag()+": dropping empty text after mention stripping",
   774	                                "message_id", messageID,
   775	                                "raw_text_len", len(textBody.Text),
   776	                                "mentions", len(mentions),
   777	                        )
   778	                        return
   779	                }
   780	                p.handler(p.dispatchPlatform(), &core.Message{
   781	                        SessionKey: sessionKey, Platform: p.platformName,
   782	                        MessageID: messageID,
   783	                        UserID:    userID, UserName: userName, ChatName: chatName,
   784	                        Content: quotedPrefix + text, ReplyCtx: rctx,
   785	                })
   786	
   787	        case "image":
   788	                var imgBody struct {
   789	                        ImageKey string `json:"image_key"`
   790	                }
   791	                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(content), &imgBody); err != nil {
   792	                        slog.Error(p.tag()+": failed to parse image content", "error", err)
   793	                        return
   794	                }
   795	                imgData, mimeType, err := p.downloadImage(messageID, imgBody.ImageKey)
   796	                if err != nil {
   797	                        slog.Error(p.tag()+": download image failed", "error", err)
   798	                        return
   799	                }
   800	                p.handler(p.dispatchPlatform(), &core.Message{
   801	                        SessionKey: sessionKey, Platform: p.platformName,
   802	                        MessageID: messageID,
   803	                        UserID:    userID, UserName: userName, ChatName: chatName,
   804	                        Images:   []core.ImageAttachment{{MimeType: mimeType, Data: imgData}},
   805	                        ReplyCtx: rctx,
   806	                })
   807	
   808	        case "audio":
   809	                var audioBody struct {
   810	                        FileKey  string `json:"file_key"`
   811	                        Duration int    `json:"duration"` // milliseconds
   812	                }
   813	                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(content), &audioBody); err != nil {
   814	                        slog.Error(p.tag()+": failed to parse audio content", "error", err)
   815	                        return
   816	                }
   817	                slog.Debug(p.tag()+": audio received", "user", userID, "file_key", audioBody.FileKey)
   818	                audioData, err := p.downloadResource(messageID, audioBody.FileKey, "file")
   819	                if err != nil {
   820	                        slog.Error(p.tag()+": download audio failed", "error", err)
   821	                        return
   822	                }
   823	                p.handler(p.dispatchPlatform(), &core.Message{
   824	                        SessionKey: sessionKey, Platform: p.platformName,
   825	                        MessageID: messageID,
   826	                        UserID:    userID, UserName: userName, ChatName: chatName,
   827	                        Audio: &core.AudioAttachment{
   828	                                MimeType: "audio/opus",
   829	                                Data:     audioData,
   830	                                Format:   "ogg",
   831	                                Duration: audioBody.Duration / 1000,
   832	                        },
   833	                        ReplyCtx: rctx,
   834	                })
   835	
   836	        case "post":
   837	                textParts, images := p.parsePostContent(messageID, content)
   838	                text := stripMentions(strings.Join(textParts, "\n"), mentions, p.botOpenID)
   839	                if text == "" && len(images) == 0 {
   840	                        return
   841	                }
   842	                p.handler(p.dispatchPlatform(), &core.Message{
   843	                        SessionKey: sessionKey, Platform: p.platformName,
   844	                        MessageID: messageID,
   845	                        UserID:    userID, UserName: userName, ChatName: chatName,
   846	                        Content: quotedPrefix + text, Images: images,
   847	                        ReplyCtx: rctx,
   848	                })
   849	
   850	        case "file":
   851	                var fileBody struct {
   852	                        FileKey  string `json:"file_key"`
   853	                        FileName string `json:"file_name"`
   854	                }
   855	                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(content), &fileBody); err != nil {
   856	                        slog.Error(p.tag()+": failed to parse file content", "error", err)
   857	                        return
   858	                }
   859	                slog.Info(p.tag()+": file received", "user", userID, "file_key", fileBody.FileKey, "file_name", fileBody.FileName)
   860	                fileData, err := p.downloadResource(messageID, fileBody.FileKey, "file")
   861	                if err != nil {
   862	                        slog.Error(p.tag()+": download file failed", "error", err)
   863	                        return
   864	                }
   865	                slog.Debug(p.tag()+": file downloaded", "file_name", fileBody.FileName, "size", len(fileData))
   866	                mimeType := detectMimeType(fileData)
   867	                p.handler(p.dispatchPlatform(), &core.Message{
   868	                        SessionKey: sessionKey, Platform: p.platformName,
   869	                        MessageID: messageID,
   870	                        UserID:    userID, UserName: userName, ChatName: chatName,
   871	                        Files: []core.FileAttachment{{
   872	                                MimeType: mimeType,
   873	                                Data:     fileData,
   874	                                FileName: fileBody.FileName,
   875	                        }},
   876	                        ReplyCtx: rctx,
   877	                })
   878	
   879	        case "merge_forward":
   880	                text, images, files := p.parseMergeForward(messageID)
   881	                if text == "" && len(images) == 0 && len(files) == 0 {
   882	                        slog.Warn(p.tag()+": merge_forward produced no content", "message_id", messageID)
   883	                        return
   884	                }
   885	                coreMsg := &core.Message{
   886	                        SessionKey: sessionKey, Platform: p.platformName,
   887	                        MessageID: messageID,
   888	                        UserID:    userID, UserName: userName, ChatName: chatName,
   889	                        Content:  text,
   890	                        Images:   images,
   891	                        Files:    files,
   892	                        ReplyCtx: rctx,
   893	                }
   894	                p.handler(p.dispatchPlatform(), coreMsg)
   895	
   896	        default:
   897	                slog.Debug(p.tag()+": ignoring unsupported message type", "type", msgType)
   898	        }
   899	}
   900

  5646	func TestQueueMessageForBusySession_FIFODequeue(t *testing.T) {
  5647	        p := &stubPlatformEngine{n: "test"}
  5648	        sess := newQueuingSession("qs1")
  5649	        agent := &controllableAgent{nextSession: sess}
  5650	        e := NewEngine("test", agent, []Platform{p}, "", LangEnglish)
  5651	
  5652	        key := "test:user1"
  5653	
  5654	        // Set up an interactive state as if a turn is in progress.
  5655	        state := &interactiveState{
  5656	                agentSession: sess,
  5657	                platform:     p,
  5658	                replyCtx:     "ctx1",
  5659	        }
  5660	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  5661	        e.interactiveStates[key] = state
  5662	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  5663	
  5664	        // Queue two messages while the session is "busy".
  5665	        msg1 := &Message{SessionKey: key, Content: "msg1", ReplyCtx: "ctx-msg1"}
  5666	        msg2 := &Message{SessionKey: key, Content: "msg2", ReplyCtx: "ctx-msg2"}
  5667	
  5668	        ok1 := e.queueMessageForBusySession(p, msg1, key)
  5669	        ok2 := e.queueMessageForBusySession(p, msg2, key)
  5670	
  5671	        if !ok1 || !ok2 {
  5672	                t.Fatal("expected both messages to be queued successfully")
  5673	        }
  5674	
  5675	        // Since deferred-send, messages are NOT sent to agent stdin at queue
  5676	        // time — only metadata is stored. Verify no Send calls occurred.
  5677	        sess.sendMu.Lock()
  5678	        if len(sess.sendCalls) != 0 {
  5679	                t.Fatalf("sendCalls = %v, want [] (deferred send)", sess.sendCalls)
  5680	        }
  5681	        sess.sendMu.Unlock()
  5682	
  5683	        // Verify pending messages queue has correct FIFO order.
  5684	        state.mu.Lock()
  5685	        if len(state.pendingMessages) != 2 {
  5686	                t.Fatalf("pendingMessages len = %d, want 2", len(state.pendingMessages))
  5687	        }
  5688	        if state.pendingMessages[0].content != "msg1" || state.pendingMessages[1].content != "msg2" {
  5689	                t.Fatalf("pendingMessages = [%s, %s], want [msg1, msg2]",
  5690	                        state.pendingMessages[0].content, state.pendingMessages[1].content)
  5691	        }
  5692	        state.mu.Unlock()
  5693	}

  5695	func TestProcessInteractiveEvents_DrainsQueuedMessages(t *testing.T) {
  5696	        p := &stubPlatformEngine{n: "test"}
  5697	        sess := newQueuingSession("qs2")
  5698	        agent := &controllableAgent{nextSession: sess}
  5699	        e := NewEngine("test", agent, []Platform{p}, "", LangEnglish)
  5700	
  5701	        key := "test:user1"
  5702	        session := e.sessions.GetOrCreateActive(key)
  5703	
  5704	        // Pre-populate the interactive state with one queued message.
  5705	        state := &interactiveState{
  5706	                agentSession: sess,
  5707	                platform:     p,
  5708	                replyCtx:     "ctx-turn1",
  5709	                pendingMessages: []queuedMessage{
  5710	                        {platform: p, replyCtx: "ctx-turn2", content: "queued-msg"},
  5711	                },
  5712	        }
  5713	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  5714	        e.interactiveStates[key] = state
  5715	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  5716	
  5717	        // Simulate the agent completing turn 1 then turn 2.
  5718	        // Turn 2 events are pushed only after Send() is called for the queued
  5719	        // message, matching real-world timing where the agent doesn't produce
  5720	        // events for a turn until it receives the prompt on stdin.
  5721	        go func() {
  5722	                // Turn 1 result
  5723	                sess.events <- Event{Type: EventText, Content: "response1"}
  5724	                sess.events <- Event{Type: EventResult, Content: "response1", Done: true}
  5725	                // Wait for the queued message's Send() call before pushing turn 2 events.
  5726	                sess.sendMu.Lock()
  5727	                for len(sess.sendCalls) == 0 {
  5728	                        sess.sendMu.Unlock()
  5729	                        time.Sleep(5 * time.Millisecond)
  5730	                        sess.sendMu.Lock()
  5731	                }
  5732	                sess.sendMu.Unlock()
  5733	                // Turn 2 result (for the queued message)
  5734	                sess.events <- Event{Type: EventText, Content: "response2"}
  5735	                sess.events <- Event{Type: EventResult, Content: "response2", Done: true}
  5736	        }()
  5737	
  5738	        session.AddHistory("user", "initial-msg")
  5739	
  5740	        sendDone := make(chan error, 1)
  5741	        sendDone <- nil
  5742	
  5743	        // processInteractiveEvents should handle both turns.
  5744	        done := make(chan struct{})
  5745	        go func() {
  5746	                e.processInteractiveEvents(state, session, e.sessions, key, "msg1", time.Now(), nil, sendDone, nil)
  5747	                close(done)
  5748	        }()
  5749	
  5750	        select {
  5751	        case <-done:
  5752	                // ok
  5753	        case <-time.After(5 * time.Second):
  5754	                t.Fatal("processInteractiveEvents did not complete in time")
  5755	        }
  5756	
  5757	        // Verify queue is empty after processing.
  5758	        state.mu.Lock()
  5759	        remaining := len(state.pendingMessages)
  5760	        state.mu.Unlock()
  5761	        if remaining != 0 {
  5762	                t.Fatalf("pendingMessages after processing = %d, want 0", remaining)
  5763	        }
  5764	
  5765	        // Verify both turns recorded in session history.
  5766	        history := session.GetHistory(100)
  5767	        var assistantMsgs []string
  5768	        for _, h := range history {
  5769	                if h.Role == "assistant" {
  5770	                        assistantMsgs = append(assistantMsgs, h.Content)
  5771	                }
  5772	        }
  5773	        if len(assistantMsgs) != 2 {
  5774	                t.Fatalf("assistant history entries = %d, want 2", len(assistantMsgs))
  5775	        }
  5776	
  5777	        // Verify the queued message was also added to history.
  5778	        var userMsgs []string
  5779	        for _, h := range history {
  5780	                if h.Role == "user" {
  5781	                        userMsgs = append(userMsgs, h.Content)
  5782	                }
  5783	        }
  5784	        if len(userMsgs) < 2 {
  5785	                t.Fatalf("user history entries = %d, want >= 2", len(userMsgs))
  5786	        }
  5787	}
  5788	
  5789	// TestDrainOrphanedQueue_UsesWorkspaceSessionManager verifies that
  5790	// drainOrphanedQueue saves session history through the passed sessions
  5791	// manager (workspace-specific) rather than e.sessions (global).
  5792	func TestDrainOrphanedQueue_UsesWorkspaceSessionManager(t *testing.T) {
  5793	        p := &stubPlatformEngine{n: "test"}
  5794	        sess := newQueuingSession("qs-orphan")
  5795	        agent := &controllableAgent{nextSession: sess}
  5796	        e := NewEngine("test", agent, []Platform{p}, "", LangEnglish)
  5797	
  5798	        // Create a separate "workspace" session manager that drainOrphanedQueue should use.
  5799	        wsSessionsPath := filepath.Join(t.TempDir(), "ws_sessions.json")
  5800	        wsSessions := NewSessionManager(wsSessionsPath)
  5801	
  5802	        key := "ws1:test:user1"
  5803	        session := wsSessions.GetOrCreateActive("test:user1")
  5804	        if !session.TryLock() {
  5805	                t.Fatal("expected TryLock to succeed")
  5806	        }
  5807	
  5808	        // Set up interactive state with a queued message.
  5809	        state := &interactiveState{
  5810	                agentSession: sess,
  5811	                platform:     p,
  5812	                replyCtx:     "ctx",
  5813	                pendingMessages: []queuedMessage{
  5814	                        {platform: p, replyCtx: "ctx-q", content: "queued-orphan"},
  5815	                },
  5816	        }
  5817	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  5818	        e.interactiveStates[key] = state
  5819	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  5820	
  5821	        // Push events so the drain completes.
  5822	        go func() {
  5823	                sess.sendMu.Lock()
  5824	                for len(sess.sendCalls) == 0 {
  5825	                        sess.sendMu.Unlock()
  5826	                        time.Sleep(5 * time.Millisecond)
  5827	                        sess.sendMu.Lock()
  5828	                }
  5829	                sess.sendMu.Unlock()
  5830	                sess.events <- Event{Type: EventResult, Content: "orphan-response", Done: true}
  5831	        }()
  5832	
  5833	        done := make(chan struct{})
  5834	        go func() {
  5835	                e.drainOrphanedQueue(session, wsSessions, key, agent, "")
  5836	                close(done)
  5837	        }()
  5838	
  5839	        select {
  5840	        case <-done:
  5841	        case <-time.After(5 * time.Second):
  5842	                t.Fatal("drainOrphanedQueue did not complete in time")
  5843	        }
  5844	
  5845	        // The assistant response should be saved in the workspace session manager,
  5846	        // NOT in e.sessions (global).
  5847	        wsHistory := wsSessions.GetOrCreateActive("test:user1").GetHistory(0)
  5848	        var wsAssistant []string
  5849	        for _, h := range wsHistory {
  5850	                if h.Role == "assistant" {
  5851	                        wsAssistant = append(wsAssistant, h.Content)
  5852	                }
  5853	        }
  5854	        if len(wsAssistant) == 0 {
  5855	                t.Fatal("expected assistant history in workspace session manager, got none")
  5856	        }
  5857	
  5858	        // Verify e.sessions (global) does NOT have this history.
  5859	        globalSession := e.sessions.GetOrCreateActive("test:user1")
  5860	        globalHistory := globalSession.GetHistory(0)
  5861	        for _, h := range globalHistory {
  5862	                if h.Role == "assistant" && h.Content == "orphan-response" {
  5863	                        t.Fatal("orphan response was saved to global e.sessions instead of workspace sessions")
  5864	                }
  5865	        }
  5866	}

   283	// StartSession creates a persistent interactive Claude Code session.
   284	func (a *Agent) StartSession(ctx context.Context, sessionID string) (core.AgentSession, error) {
   285	        a.mu.Lock()
   286	        tools := make([]string, len(a.allowedTools))
   287	        copy(tools, a.allowedTools)
   288	        disTools := make([]string, len(a.disallowedTools))
   289	        copy(disTools, a.disallowedTools)
   290	        maxTok := a.maxContextTokens
   291	        model := a.model
   292	        extraEnv := a.providerEnvLocked()
   293	        extraEnv = append(extraEnv, a.sessionEnv...)
   294	
   295	        // Add Claude Code Router environment variables if configured
   296	        if a.routerURL != "" {
   297	                extraEnv = append(extraEnv, "ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="+a.routerURL)
   298	                // When using router, we need to prevent proxy interference
   299	                extraEnv = append(extraEnv, "NO_PROXY=127.0.0.1")
   300	                // Disable telemetry and cost warnings for cleaner router integration
   301	                extraEnv = append(extraEnv, "DISABLE_TELEMETRY=true")
   302	                extraEnv = append(extraEnv, "DISABLE_COST_WARNINGS=true")
   303	        }
   304	        if a.routerAPIKey != "" {
   305	                extraEnv = append(extraEnv, "ANTHROPIC_API_KEY="+a.routerAPIKey)
   306	        }
   307	
   308	        if a.activeIdx >= 0 && a.activeIdx < len(a.providers) {
   309	                if m := a.providers[a.activeIdx].Model; m != "" {
   310	                        model = m
   311	                }
   312	        }
   313	        platformPrompt := a.platformPrompt
   314	        // When router_url is set, --verbose conflicts with --output-format stream-json
   315	        // (verbose emits non-JSON text to stdout that corrupts the JSON stream).
   316	        disableVerbose := a.routerURL != ""
   317	        a.mu.Unlock()
   318	
   319	        return newClaudeSession(ctx, a.workDir, model, sessionID, a.mode, tools, disTools, extraEnv, platformPrompt, disableVerbose, a.spawnOpts, maxTok)
   320	}

  6005	func TestQueueMessageOverflow_DropsOldestAndReturnsfalse(t *testing.T) {
  6006	        p := &stubPlatformEngine{n: "test"}
  6007	        sess := newQueuingSession("qs-overflow")
  6008	        agent := &controllableAgent{nextSession: sess}
  6009	        e := NewEngine("test", agent, []Platform{p}, "", LangEnglish)
  6010	
  6011	        key := "test:overflow-user"
  6012	
  6013	        state := &interactiveState{
  6014	                agentSession: sess,
  6015	                platform:     p,
  6016	                replyCtx:     "ctx",
  6017	        }
  6018	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  6019	        e.interactiveStates[key] = state
  6020	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  6021	
  6022	        // Fill the queue to maxQueuedMessages (5).
  6023	        for i := 0; i < maxQueuedMessages; i++ {
  6024	                msg := &Message{SessionKey: key, Content: fmt.Sprintf("msg-%d", i), ReplyCtx: fmt.Sprintf("ctx-%d", i)}
  6025	                ok := e.queueMessageForBusySession(p, msg, key)
  6026	                if !ok {
  6027	                        t.Fatalf("expected msg-%d to be queued, got false", i)
  6028	                }
  6029	        }
  6030	
  6031	        state.mu.Lock()
  6032	        if len(state.pendingMessages) != maxQueuedMessages {
  6033	                t.Fatalf("queue depth = %d, want %d", len(state.pendingMessages), maxQueuedMessages)
  6034	        }
  6035	        state.mu.Unlock()
  6036	
  6037	        // The 6th message should be rejected (returns false).
  6038	        overflow := &Message{SessionKey: key, Content: "msg-overflow", ReplyCtx: "ctx-overflow"}
  6039	        ok := e.queueMessageForBusySession(p, overflow, key)
  6040	        if ok {
  6041	                t.Fatal("expected 6th message to be rejected (queue full)")
  6042	        }
  6043	
  6044	        // Queue should still have exactly maxQueuedMessages items (the original 5).
  6045	        state.mu.Lock()
  6046	        if len(state.pendingMessages) != maxQueuedMessages {
  6047	                t.Fatalf("queue depth after overflow = %d, want %d", len(state.pendingMessages), maxQueuedMessages)
  6048	        }
  6049	        // First message should still be msg-0 (FIFO preserved, no silent drop).
  6050	        if state.pendingMessages[0].content != "msg-0" {
  6051	                t.Fatalf("first queued = %q, want msg-0", state.pendingMessages[0].content)
  6052	        }
  6053	        state.mu.Unlock()
  6054	
  6055	        // Platform should have received the MsgMessageQueued replies for the 5 accepted + nothing for rejected.
  6056	        sent := p.getSent()
  6057	        if len(sent) != maxQueuedMessages {
  6058	                t.Fatalf("platform replies = %d, want %d (one per accepted queue)", len(sent), maxQueuedMessages)
  6059	        }
  6060	}

    25	// claudeSession manages a long-running Claude Code process using
    26	// --input-format stream-json and --permission-prompt-tool stdio.
    27	//
    28	// In "auto" mode, permission requests are auto-approved internally
    29	// (avoiding --dangerously-skip-permissions which fails under root).
    30	type claudeSession struct {
    31	        cmd             *exec.Cmd
    32	        stdin           io.WriteCloser
    33	        stdinMu         sync.Mutex
    34	        events          chan core.Event
    35	        sessionID       atomic.Value // stores string
    36	        permissionMode  atomic.Value // stores string
    37	        autoApprove     atomic.Bool
    38	        acceptEditsOnly atomic.Bool
    39	        dontAsk         atomic.Bool
    40	        workDir         string
    41	        ctx             context.Context
    42	        cancel          context.CancelFunc
    43	        done            chan struct{}
    44	        alive           atomic.Bool
    45	
    46	        // gracefulStopTimeout is how long Close() waits for a clean exit
    47	        // (stdin close → Stop hooks → process exit) before escalating to
    48	        // SIGTERM and then SIGKILL. Default: 120s to match claude-mem's
    49	        // Stop hook timeout. The wait ends as soon as the process exits,
    50	        // so typical shutdowns take seconds, not the full timeout.
    51	        gracefulStopTimeout time.Duration
    52	}
    53	
    54	func newClaudeSession(ctx context.Context, workDir, model, sessionID, mode string, allowedTools, disallowedTools []string, extraEnv []string, platformPrompt string, disableVerbose bool, spawnOpts core.SpawnOptions, maxContextTokens int) (*claudeSession, error) {
    55	        sessionCtx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)
    56	
    57	        args := []string{
    58	                "--output-format", "stream-json",
    59	                "--input-format", "stream-json",
    60	                "--permission-prompt-tool", "stdio",
    61	        }
    62	        if !disableVerbose {
    63	                args = append(args, "--verbose")
    64	        }
    65	
    66	        if mode != "" && mode != "default" {
    67	                args = append(args, "--permission-mode", mode)
    68	        }
    69	        switch sessionID {
    70	        case "":
    71	                // Truly fresh session — no resume, no continue.
    72	        case core.ContinueSession:
    73	                // --continue grabs the most recent session in the workspace, which
    74	                // may belong to an active CLI terminal. Fork it so the platform
    75	                // conversation gets its own independent context branch.
    76	                args = append(args, "--continue", "--fork-session")
    77	        default:
    78	                // Resuming a known session ID — this is cc-connect's own session
    79	                // from a previous connection, safe to resume directly.
    80	                args = append(args, "--resume", sessionID)
    81	        }
    82	        if model != "" {
    83	                args = append(args, "--model", model)
    84	        }
    85	        if len(allowedTools) > 0 {
    86	                args = append(args, "--allowedTools", strings.Join(allowedTools, ","))
    87	        }
    88	        if len(disallowedTools) > 0 {
    89	                args = append(args, "--disallowedTools", strings.Join(disallowedTools, ","))
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        if sysPrompt := core.AgentSystemPrompt(); sysPrompt != "" {
    93	                if platformPrompt != "" {
    94	                        sysPrompt += "\n## Formatting\n" + platformPrompt + "\n"
    95	                }
    96	                args = append(args, "--append-system-prompt", sysPrompt)
    97	        }
    98	
    99	        if maxContextTokens > 0 {
   100	                args = append(args, "--max-context-tokens", strconv.Itoa(maxContextTokens))
   101	        }
   102	
   103	        slog.Debug("claudeSession: starting", "args", core.RedactArgs(args), "dir", workDir, "mode", mode, "run_as_user", spawnOpts.RunAsUser)
   104	
   105	        // Per-spawn defense in depth: if run_as_user is set, re-run the cheap
   106	        // preflight (sudo still works + target still can't escalate) right
   107	        // before we build the command. This catches sudoers being edited
   108	        // between startup preflight and now.
   109	        if spawnOpts.IsolationMode() {
   110	                verifyCtx, verifyCancel := context.WithTimeout(sessionCtx, 10*time.Second)
   111	                err := core.VerifyRunAsUserCheap(verifyCtx, core.ExecSudoRunner{}, spawnOpts.RunAsUser)
   112	                verifyCancel()
   113	                if err != nil {
   114	                        cancel()
   115	                        return nil, fmt.Errorf("claudeSession: run_as_user spawn refused: %w", err)

   172	
   173	func (cs *claudeSession) readLoop(stdout io.ReadCloser, stderrBuf *bytes.Buffer) {
   174	        defer func() {
   175	                cs.alive.Store(false)
   176	                if err := cs.cmd.Wait(); err != nil {
   177	                        stderrMsg := strings.TrimSpace(stderrBuf.String())
   178	                        if stderrMsg != "" {
   179	                                slog.Error("claudeSession: process failed", "error", err, "stderr", stderrMsg)
   180	                                evt := core.Event{Type: core.EventError, Error: fmt.Errorf("%s", stderrMsg)}
   181	                                select {
   182	                                case cs.events <- evt:
   183	                                case <-cs.ctx.Done():
   184	                                        return
   185	                                }
   186	                        }
   187	                }
   188	                close(cs.events)
   189	                close(cs.done)
   190	        }()
   191	
   192	        scanner := bufio.NewScanner(stdout)
   193	        scanner.Buffer(make([]byte, 0, 64*1024), 10*1024*1024)
   194	
   195	        for scanner.Scan() {
   196	                line := scanner.Text()
   197	                if line == "" {
   198	                        continue
   199	                }
   200	
   201	                var raw map[string]any
   202	                if err := json.Unmarshal([]byte(line), &raw); err != nil {
   203	                        slog.Debug("claudeSession: non-JSON line", "line", line)
   204	                        continue
   205	                }
   206	
   207	                eventType, _ := raw["type"].(string)
   208	                slog.Debug("claudeSession: event", "type", eventType)
   209	
   210	                switch eventType {
   211	                case "system":
   212	                        cs.handleSystem(raw)
   213	                case "assistant":
   214	                        cs.handleAssistant(raw)
   215	                case "user":
   216	                        cs.handleUser(raw)
   217	                case "result":
   218	                        cs.handleResult(raw)
   219	                case "control_request":
   220	                        cs.handleControlRequest(raw)
   221	                case "control_cancel_request":
   222	                        requestID, _ := raw["request_id"].(string)
   223	                        slog.Debug("claudeSession: permission cancelled", "request_id", requestID)
   224	                }
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        if err := scanner.Err(); err != nil {
   228	                slog.Error("claudeSession: scanner error", "error", err)
   229	                evt := core.Event{Type: core.EventError, Error: fmt.Errorf("read stdout: %w", err)}
   230	                select {

   419	// Send writes a user message (with optional images and files) to the Claude process stdin.
   420	// Images are sent as base64 in the multimodal content array.
   421	// Files are saved to local temp files and referenced in the text prompt
   422	// so Claude Code can read them with its built-in tools.
   423	func (cs *claudeSession) Send(prompt string, images []core.ImageAttachment, files []core.FileAttachment) error {
   424	        if !cs.alive.Load() {
   425	                return fmt.Errorf("session process is not running")
   426	        }
   427	
   428	        if len(images) == 0 && len(files) == 0 {
   429	                return cs.writeJSON(map[string]any{
   430	                        "type":    "user",
   431	                        "message": map[string]any{"role": "user", "content": prompt},
   432	                })
   433	        }
   434	
   435	        attachDir := filepath.Join(cs.workDir, ".cc-connect", "attachments")
   436	        if err := os.MkdirAll(attachDir, 0o755); err != nil {
   437	                slog.Warn("claudeSession: mkdir attachments failed", "error", err, "path", attachDir)
   438	        }
   439	
   440	        var parts []map[string]any
   441	        var savedPaths []string
   442	
   443	        // Save and encode images
   444	        for i, img := range images {
   445	                ext := extFromMime(img.MimeType)
   446	                fname := fmt.Sprintf("img_%d_%d%s", time.Now().UnixMilli(), i, ext)
   447	                fpath := filepath.Join(attachDir, fname)
   448	                if err := os.WriteFile(fpath, img.Data, 0o644); err != nil {
   449	                        slog.Error("claudeSession: save image failed", "error", err)
   450	                        continue
   451	                }
   452	                savedPaths = append(savedPaths, fpath)
   453	                slog.Debug("claudeSession: image saved", "path", fpath, "size", len(img.Data))
   454	
   455	                mimeType := img.MimeType
   456	                if mimeType == "" {
   457	                        mimeType = "image/png"
   458	                }
   459	                parts = append(parts, map[string]any{
   460	                        "type": "image",
   461	                        "source": map[string]any{
   462	                                "type":       "base64",
   463	                                "media_type": mimeType,
   464	                                "data":       base64.StdEncoding.EncodeToString(img.Data),
   465	                        },
   466	                })
   467	        }
   468	
   469	        // Save files to disk so Claude Code can read them
   470	        filePaths := core.SaveFilesToDisk(cs.workDir, files)

     8	// Platform abstracts a messaging platform (Feishu, DingTalk, Slack, etc.).
     9	type Platform interface {
    10	        Name() string
    11	        Start(handler MessageHandler) error
    12	        Reply(ctx context.Context, replyCtx any, content string) error
    13	        Send(ctx context.Context, replyCtx any, content string) error
    14	        Stop() error
    15	}

    17	// ErrNotSupported indicates a platform doesn't support a particular operation.
    18	var ErrNotSupported = errors.New("operation not supported by this platform")
    19	
    20	// ReplyContextReconstructor is an optional interface for platforms that can
    21	// recreate a reply context from a session key. This is needed for cron jobs
    22	// to send messages to users without an incoming message.
    23	type ReplyContextReconstructor interface {
    24	        ReconstructReplyCtx(sessionKey string) (any, error)
    25	}
    26	
    27	// CronReplyTargetResolver is an optional interface for platforms that need to
    28	// map a logical cron session key to the actual reply target used at execution
    29	// time. This is useful for platforms where proactive replies may need to create
    30	// or switch to a thread before the cron run starts.
    31	//
    32	// Implementations that do not need special handling should return
    33	// ErrNotSupported so callers can fall back to ReconstructReplyCtx(sessionKey).
    34	type CronReplyTargetResolver interface {
    35	        ResolveCronReplyTarget(sessionKey string, title string) (resolvedSessionKey string, replyCtx any, err error)
    36	}

    58	// AgentSystemPrompt returns the system prompt fragment that informs agents about
    59	// cc-connect capabilities (cron scheduling, etc.).
    60	// The prompt is designed to be appended to the agent's existing system prompt.
    61	func AgentSystemPrompt() string {
    62	        return `You are running inside cc-connect, a bridge that connects you to messaging platforms.
    63	Your normal text responses are automatically delivered to the user — just reply normally, do NOT use cc-connect send for ordinary text replies.
    64	
    65	## Available tools
    66	
    67	### Send generated images or files back to the user
    68	When you generate a local image or file that should be sent to the user, use:
    69	
    70	  cc-connect send --image /absolute/path/to/image.png
    71	  cc-connect send --file /absolute/path/to/report.pdf
    72	  cc-connect send --file /absolute/path/to/report.pdf --image /absolute/path/to/chart.png
    73	
    74	You may repeat --image / --file multiple times. Use this only for generated attachments that need to be delivered to the user.
    75	If you include --message, do not repeat the exact same sentence again in your normal reply, because your normal reply is also delivered automatically.
    76	
    77	### Scheduled tasks (cron)
    78	When the user asks you to do something on a schedule (e.g. "每天早上6点帮我总结GitHub trending"), use the Bash tool to run:
    79	
    80	  cc-connect cron add --cron "<min> <hour> <day> <month> <weekday>" --prompt "<task description>" --desc "<short label>"
    81	
    82	Environment variables CC_PROJECT and CC_SESSION_KEY are already set, so you do NOT need to specify --project or --session-key.
    83	
    84	Optional flags:
    85	  --session-mode <mode>     reuse (default) or new-per-run (fresh session each trigger)
    86	  --timeout-mins <n>        max wait per run in minutes (default 30, 0 = unlimited)
    87	  --exec <command>          run a shell command directly instead of --prompt
    88	
    89	Examples:
    90	  cc-connect cron add --cron "0 6 * * *" --prompt "Collect GitHub trending repos and send a summary" --desc "Daily GitHub Trending"
    91	  cc-connect cron add --cron "0 9 * * 1" --prompt "Generate a weekly project status report" --desc "Weekly Report"
    92	  cc-connect cron add --cron "*/2 * * * *" --exec "ipconfig" --session-mode new-per-run --desc "Every 2 min ipconfig"
    93	
    94	You can also list or delete cron jobs:
    95	  cc-connect cron list
    96	  cc-connect cron del <job-id>
    97	
    98	### Bot-to-bot relay
    99	When you need to communicate with another bot (e.g. ask another AI agent a question), use:
   100	
   101	  cc-connect relay send --to <target_project> "<message>"
   102	
   103	IMPORTANT: <target_project> must be the EXACT project name from the /bind command output.
   104	Do NOT guess or modify the name — use it exactly as shown (e.g. "gemini", not "gemini-bot").
   105	
   106	This sends a message to the target bot and waits for its response (printed to stdout).
   107	The conversation is visible in the group chat and each bot maintains its own relay session.
   108	
   109	Environment variables CC_PROJECT and CC_SESSION_KEY are already set, so the relay knows which group chat to use.
   110	`
   111	}

   190	// recoverable platforms.
   191	type PlatformLifecycleHandler interface {
   192	        OnPlatformReady(p Platform)
   193	        OnPlatformUnavailable(p Platform, err error)
   194	}
   195	
   196	// AsyncRecoverablePlatform is an optional interface for platforms that start
   197	// a background recovery loop and later report readiness or unavailability.
   198	//
   199	// Platforms implementing this interface may return from Start() before they are
   200	// actually ready to receive traffic. Callers must treat OnPlatformReady as the
   201	// signal that deferred platform capabilities may be initialized and the
   202	// platform is usable. A nil Start() return therefore means the recovery loop
   203	// was launched successfully, not necessarily that an initial connection was
   204	// established.
   205	type AsyncRecoverablePlatform interface {
   206	        Platform
   207	        SetLifecycleHandler(h PlatformLifecycleHandler)
   208	}
   209	
   210	// MessageHandler is called by platforms when a new message arrives.
   211	type MessageHandler func(p Platform, msg *Message)
   212	
   213	// Agent abstracts an AI coding assistant (Claude Code, Cursor, Gemini CLI, etc.).
   214	// All agents must support persistent bidirectional sessions via StartSession.
   215	type Agent interface {
   216	        Name() string
   217	        // StartSession creates or resumes an interactive session with a persistent process.
   218	        StartSession(ctx context.Context, sessionID string) (AgentSession, error)
   219	        // ListSessions returns sessions known to the agent backend.
   220	        ListSessions(ctx context.Context) ([]AgentSessionInfo, error)
   221	        Stop() error
   222	}
   223	
   224	// AgentSession represents a running interactive agent session with a persistent process.
   225	type AgentSession interface {
   226	        // Send sends a user message (with optional images and files) to the running agent process.
   227	        Send(prompt string, images []ImageAttachment, files []FileAttachment) error
   228	        // RespondPermission sends a permission decision back to the agent process.
   229	        RespondPermission(requestID string, result PermissionResult) error
   230	        // Events returns the channel that emits agent events (kept open across turns).
   231	        Events() <-chan Event
   232	        // CurrentSessionID returns the current agent-side session ID.
   233	        CurrentSessionID() string
   234	        // Alive returns true if the underlying process is still running.
   235	        Alive() bool
   236	        // Close terminates the session and its underlying process.
   237	        Close() error
   238	}
   239	
   240	// PermissionResult represents the user's decision on a permission request.
   241	type PermissionResult struct {
   242	        Behavior     string         `json:"behavior"`               // "allow" or "deny"
   243	        UpdatedInput map[string]any `json:"updatedInput,omitempty"` // echoed back for allow
   244	        Message      string         `json:"message,omitempty"`      // reason for deny
   245	}

  5345	// blockingSendAgentSession blocks in Send until unblock is closed, mimicking agents
  5346	// whose Send does not return until the prompt turn completes (e.g. ACP session/prompt).
  5347	type blockingSendAgentSession struct {
  5348	        controllableAgentSession
  5349	        sendStarted chan struct{} // sent to when Send begins waiting on unblock
  5350	        unblock     chan struct{} // close to let Send return
  5351	}
  5352	
  5353	func newBlockingSendSession(id string) *blockingSendAgentSession {
  5354	        return &blockingSendAgentSession{
  5355	                controllableAgentSession: controllableAgentSession{
  5356	                        sessionID: id,
  5357	                        alive:     true,
  5358	                        events:    make(chan Event, 16),
  5359	                        closed:    make(chan struct{}),
  5360	                },
  5361	                sendStarted: make(chan struct{}, 1),
  5362	                unblock:     make(chan struct{}),
  5363	        }
  5364	}
  5365	
  5366	func (s *blockingSendAgentSession) Send(_ string, _ []ImageAttachment, _ []FileAttachment) error {
  5367	        s.sendStarted <- struct{}{}
  5368	        <-s.unblock
  5369	        return nil
  5370	}

package core

import (
    "context"
    "runtime"
    "strings"
    "sync"
    "testing"
    "time"
)

type reproPlatform struct{ sent []string; mu sync.Mutex }
func (p *reproPlatform) Name() string { return "repro" }
func (p *reproPlatform) Start(MessageHandler) error { return nil }
func (p *reproPlatform) Reply(_ context.Context, _ any, content string) error { p.mu.Lock(); defer p.mu.Unlock(); p.sent = append(p.sent, content); return nil }
func (p *reproPlatform) Send(_ context.Context, _ any, content string) error { return p.Reply(context.Background(), nil, content) }
func (p *reproPlatform) Stop() error { return nil }
func (p *reproPlatform) has(substr string) bool { p.mu.Lock(); defer p.mu.Unlock(); for _, s := range p.sent { if strings.Contains(s, substr) { return true } }; return false }

type reproAgent struct{ sess *reproSession }
func (a *reproAgent) Name() string { return "repro-agent" }
func (a *reproAgent) StartSession(context.Context, string) (AgentSession, error) { if a.sess == nil { a.sess = &reproSession{events: make(chan Event, 8), alive: true} }; return a.sess, nil }
func (a *reproAgent) ListSessions(context.Context) ([]AgentSessionInfo, error) { return nil, nil }
func (a *reproAgent) Stop() error { return nil }

type reproSession struct{ events chan Event; alive bool }
func (s *reproSession) Send(string, []ImageAttachment, []FileAttachment) error { return nil }
func (s *reproSession) RespondPermission(string, PermissionResult) error { return nil }
func (s *reproSession) Events() <-chan Event { return s.events }
func (s *reproSession) CurrentSessionID() string { return "sid" }
func (s *reproSession) Alive() bool { return s.alive }
func (s *reproSession) Close() error { s.alive = false; close(s.events); return nil }

func TestReproSecondMessageBeforeInteractiveStateIsDropped(t *testing.T) {
    old := runtime.GOMAXPROCS(1)
    defer runtime.GOMAXPROCS(old)
    p := &reproPlatform{}
    a := &reproAgent{}
    e := NewEngine("repro", a, []Platform{p}, "", LangEnglish)
    key := "repro:user"
    e.handleMessage(p, &Message{SessionKey: key, Platform: "repro", MessageID: "m1", Content: "first", ReplyCtx: "c1"})
    e.handleMessage(p, &Message{SessionKey: key, Platform: "repro", MessageID: "m2", Content: "second", ReplyCtx: "c2"})
    time.Sleep(50*time.Millisecond)
    if p.has(e.i18n.T(MsgPreviousProcessing)) {
        t.Fatalf("second message was not queued; got previous-processing reply")
    }
}
EOF

  1576	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  1577	        state, hasState := e.interactiveStates[interactiveKey]

package core

import (
    "context"
    "runtime"
    "strings"
    "sync"
    "testing"
    "time"
)

type reproPlatform struct{ sent []string; mu sync.Mutex }
func (p *reproPlatform) Name() string { return "repro" }
func (p *reproPlatform) Start(MessageHandler) error { return nil }
func (p *reproPlatform) Reply(_ context.Context, _ any, content string) error { p.mu.Lock(); defer p.mu.Unlock(); p.sent = append(p.sent, content); return nil }
func (p *reproPlatform) Send(_ context.Context, _ any, content string) error { return p.Reply(context.Background(), nil, content) }
func (p *reproPlatform) Stop() error { return nil }
func (p *reproPlatform) has(substr string) bool { p.mu.Lock(); defer p.mu.Unlock(); for _, s := range p.sent { if strings.Contains(s, substr) { return true } }; return false }

type reproAgent struct{ sess *reproSession }
func (a *reproAgent) Name() string { return "repro-agent" }
func (a *reproAgent) StartSession(context.Context, string) (AgentSession, error) { if a.sess == nil { a.sess = &reproSession{events: make(chan Event, 8), alive: true} }; return a.sess, nil }
func (a *reproAgent) ListSessions(context.Context) ([]AgentSessionInfo, error) { return nil, nil }
func (a *reproAgent) Stop() error { return nil }

type reproSession struct{ events chan Event; alive bool }
func (s *reproSession) Send(string, []ImageAttachment, []FileAttachment) error { return nil }
func (s *reproSession) RespondPermission(string, PermissionResult) error { return nil }
func (s *reproSession) Events() <-chan Event { return s.events }
func (s *reproSession) CurrentSessionID() string { return "sid" }
func (s *reproSession) Alive() bool { return s.alive }
func (s *reproSession) Close() error { s.alive = false; close(s.events); return nil }

func TestReproSecondMessageBeforeInteractiveStateIsDropped(t *testing.T) {
    old := runtime.GOMAXPROCS(1)
    defer runtime.GOMAXPROCS(old)
    p := &reproPlatform{}
    a := &reproAgent{}
    e := NewEngine("repro", a, []Platform{p}, "", LangEnglish)
    key := "repro:user"
    e.handleMessage(p, &Message{SessionKey: key, Platform: "repro", MessageID: "m1", Content: "first", ReplyCtx: "c1"})
    e.handleMessage(p, &Message{SessionKey: key, Platform: "repro", MessageID: "m2", Content: "second", ReplyCtx: "c2"})
    time.Sleep(50*time.Millisecond)
    if p.has(e.i18n.T(MsgPreviousProcessing)) {
        t.Fatalf("second message was not queued; got previous-processing reply")
    }
}
EOF
cd /testbed && go test ./core -run TestReproSecondMessageBeforeInteractiveStateIsDropped -count=1
status=$?
rm -f /testbed/core/repro_queue_race_test.go
exit $status

  1576	}
  1577	
  1578	// queueMessageForBusySession queues a message for later delivery when the
  1579	// session is busy. The message is NOT sent to agent stdin at queue time;
  1580	// the event loop sends it after the current turn's EventResult is received.
  1581	// Returns true if the message was successfully queued, false otherwise.
  1582	func (e *Engine) queueMessageForBusySession(p Platform, msg *Message, interactiveKey string) bool {
  1583	        e.interactiveMu.Lock()
  1584	        state, hasState := e.interactiveStates[interactiveKey]
  1585	        e.interactiveMu.Unlock()
  1586	
  1587	        if !hasState || state == nil {
  1588	                return false
  1589	        }
  1590	        if state.agentSession == nil {
  1591	                state.mu.Lock()
  1592	                starting := state.starting
  1593	                state.mu.Unlock()
  1594	                if !starting {
  1595	                        return false
  1596	                }
  1597	        } else if !state.agentSession.Alive() {
  1598	                return false
  1599	        }
  1600	
  1601	        // Only queue metadata — do NOT send to agent stdin yet.
  1602	        // The agent CLI may treat a mid-turn stdin message as part of the
  1603	        // current turn, causing the event loop to hang waiting for a second
  1604	        // EventResult that never arrives. Instead, the event loop sends the
  1605	        // message after the current turn's EventResult is received.
  1606	        state.mu.Lock()
  1607	        if len(state.pendingMessages) >= maxQueuedMessages {
  1608	                state.mu.Unlock()
  1609	                return false // fall back to "previous processing" reply
  1610	        }
  1611	        state.pendingMessages = append(state.pendingMessages, queuedMessage{
  1612	                platform:      p,
  1613	                replyCtx:      msg.ReplyCtx,
  1614	                content:       msg.Content,
  1615	                images:        msg.Images,
  1616	                files:         msg.Files,
  1617	                fromVoice:     msg.FromVoice,
  1618	                userID:        msg.UserID,
  1619	                msgPlatform:   msg.Platform,
  1620	                msgSessionKey: msg.SessionKey,
  1621	        })
  1622	        queueDepth := len(state.pendingMessages)
  1623	        state.mu.Unlock()
  1624	
  1625	        slog.Info("message queued for busy session",
